 se zyada keemat kii sampatti ke malikana haq par jang chhidi hui he, jinamein ek teen sitara heritage hotel he, jaipur kaa khetadi house he or shahar main pahari par sthit gopalgarh kaa kila he jo laavaaris padaa hua he (shahi sampatti kii suchi ke liye dekhen box)
 All this property has been under the patronage of the state since the death of Rai Bahadur Sardar Singh, the last ruler of Khetri in 1987
 sardaar singh talakshuda the jinka koi baccha nahin tha, jisaki vajah se unke nidhan ke baad rajya sarkaar ko 1956 main banaaya gaya lekin shaayad hi kabhi istemaal kiya kanoon rajasthan aschits regulation act lagu karnaa padaa or uttaradhikari ke abhaav main sari property par kabja lenaa padaa
 The legal battle has been going on since then
 yah ladaai teen pakshon ke bich he—ek khetadi trust he jise sardaar singh ke vasietname ke hisaab se banaaya gaya tha or trust kii website ke mutabik shiksha or anusandhan kaaryon ke liye sari property vasiyat main use de di gai thi
 The second party belongs to the family of Sardar Singh in the absence of a legal heir and the third party belongs to the state
 is riyasat se apni nikatataa kaa daawa karne waalon ko haalanki adaalaton main bahut kamyaabi nahin mili he
 In 2012, giving a big blow to the Khetri Trust, the Delhi High Court ruled against its 1987 petition, which had asked the government to give all the royal property to it
 yachika par 30 saal ke dauraan 25 jajon ne sunwaayee kii or ant main sardaar singh ke 1985 ke vasietname kii kanoonee vaidhata par faisla dete hue adaalat ne kaha ki use vasietname kii asaliyat par shaq he
 The trust's appeal against this decision was approved by a bench but it will take many more years to come to a decision on it
 november 2012 main rajasthan hycourt ne alsisar ke gaj singh kii yachika ko khaarij kar diya tha, jinhone daawa kiya tha ki ve sardaar singh ke dattak putr hone ke naate uttaradhikari hai
 He even claimed that in April 1987, after the death of Sardar Singh, he performed the traditional 'pag Dastur' (tradition of nominating heirs)
 hycourt ke do nyaayadhishon kii khandpeeth ne haalanki agle saal isamen sanshodhan kar daalaa, jiske baad july 2014 main jaipur ke colector krishna kunal ne khetadi kii sampatti par kanoonee uttaradhikariyon ke daavon ko daakhil kiye jane ke liye unhen notice jari kiya
 This list of cases also left Ramakrishna Ashram untouched, which in 1958 Sardar Singh donated a grand building and many other facilities in memory of his grandfather Ajit Singh Bahadur and Swami Vivekananda to open the first center of the ashram in Rajasthan

 The trust was later returned to his office with all the belongings
 is mukademebaaji kaa jahaan koi ant hota nahin dikhataa, vahiin gaj singh kehete hai ki agar khetadi kii shahi sampatti trust ko de di jaae to unhen isamen koi dikkat nahin hogi
 But they definitely say, "if the other claimant or the government claims its ownership, then i will also submit my claim
 ” adalati faisle se lage jatke se trustee ab bhi ubar nahin paae hai

 "they indicate that they are not going to get any financial or other benefit from it anyway
 ve kehete hai ki dikkat isliye bad jaati he kyonki tatkaaleen shahi parivaar ke malikana haq vaali vibhinn chal sampatti kii suchi nadaarad he

 a member of the erstwhile royal family told India Today that a few years ago he got an offer to buy the precious sword of the Khetri princely state

 yahaan aane vaale sailaani iske chitron, shilpon or kaanch ke kaam ke saath chhedchhad karte hai
